Param/Value/lib_DA0A55AD_B178C521=Marine-class power armor was the first power armor produced by Blizzard Enforcement with ultra-ancient science and technology. Its power source was the nuclear battery, and its performance had gone through the test of wars and was very stable and reliable. <n/>The name of "Marine Corps" reflects the developers' desire to use this power armor as the standard military equipment. <n/><n/>It is divided into three models. <n/><n/>Marine-A was the first batch of stereotyped power armor with general purpose. This armor had been delivered to the US military and put into mass production. Ordinary soldiers could use Marine-A in fight after certain training. Marine-A was not equipped with fixed armor. The armor itself could provide the power equivalent to five times of that of ordinary humans, and thus it could use vehicle-mounted weapons as individual equipment. Captain Blizzard is also equipped with Marine-A. <n/><n/>Marine-B was based on Marine-A. It was a result of modifying the armor’s internal part. Part of the armor was replaced by soft materials to increase comfort, so users could wear it for a long time. Marine-B was produced with a small quantity. It was mainly supplied to special task departments and officers. <n/><n/>Marine-C was the heavy-duty type which strengthened the structural strength of joints without modifying the armor itself and was equipped with a more powerful nuclear battery. It could play the power as many as eight times of that of ordinary humans and use more large-scale weapons, such as vehicle-mounted revolving guns. However, Marine-C armor was mainly used in the construction of fortifications. Marine-C armor provided to the troops was generally equipped with large excavators and pile drivers for rapid construction of the field base. Marine-C armor was also the design blueprint of the armor Marauder.
